TITLE       U-235(n,f) cross section measurements and             21522  1    3

AUTHOR     (C.Wagemans,G.Coddens,A.J.Deruytter)                   21522  1    5 
REFERENCE  (C,79KNOX,,961,1979) Description of experiment.        21522  1    6 
            The data of this reference are superseded by          21522  1    7 
           (W,WAGEMANS,198206) Corrected pointwise cross-         21522  1    8 
            section data on magnetic tape. In fact an error       21522  1    9 
            was found in the original data sent to the NEA        21522  1   10 
            Data Bank in 1980, due to an error in the             21522  1   11 
            integration procedure used in the analysis            21522  1   12 
            code package ANGELA.                                  21522  1   13 
           (W,WAGEMANS,19800131) Data on magnetic tape, superseded21522  1   14 
INSTITUTE  (2ZZZGEL) Experimental site.                           21522  1   15 
           (2BLGMOL) First two authors.                           21522  1   16 
           (2BLGGHT) All authors.                                 21522  1   17 
FACILITY   (LINAC,2ZZZGEL) 100 MeV electron Linac accelerator     21522  1   18 
            Gelina of the CBNM.                                   21522  1   19 
INC-SOURCE (PHOTO) Using an uranium target with a polyethylene    21522  1   20 
            moderator, more details see REL-REF.                  21522  1   21 
REL-REF    (I,20826001,C.Wagemans+,J,ANE,3,437,1976) -  details   21522  1   22 
            about incident source                                 21522  1   23 
SAMPLE      U-235, 2 mg/cm*cm layer of uranylacetate, prepared    21522  1   24 
            by electrospraying on an Al-disk. Isotopic enrichment 21522  1   25 
            of 99.5%.                                             21522  1   26 
            B-10, 184 micro-grams/cm*cm layer, prepared by        21522  1   27 
            evaporating elemental boron in vacuum, isotopic       21522  1   28 
            enrichment 93.%.                                      21522  1   29 
            Li-6, 176 micro-grams/cm*cm layer, prepared by        21522  1   30 
            evaporating Li-6-F in vacuum, isotopic enrichment     21522  1   31 
            99.32%.                                               21522  1   32 
METHOD     (TOF) Time of flight spectra measured. Back-to-        21522  1   33 
            back foils of U-235 and Li-6 or B-10 (flux monitors), 21522  1   34 
            at 45. degr. With respect to the neutron beam.        21522  1   35 
            The shape of the U-235 cross section is determined    21522  1   36 
            assuming a 1/V-shape for the Li-6 or B-10 cross       21522  1   37 
            sections. Four measurements were done:                21522  1   38 
            (1.) using B-10, Linac 30 ns, 100 Hz, flight path     21522  1   39 
             7.757 m, filters Mn (permanent), Cd (background-1),  21522  1   40 
             Rh,W,Pd,Co (background-2).                           21522  1   41 
            (2.) same as (1.) but Li-6 instead of B-10.           21522  1   42 
            (3.) using Li-6, Linac 24 ns, 100 Hz, flight path     21522  1   43 
             9.450 m, filters Co,Cd (background-1), Co,W,Au,Rh,   21522  1   44 
             Mn (background-2), no permanent filter.              21522  1   45 
            (4.) Using B-10, Linac 20 ns, 400 Hz, flight path     21522  1   46 
             30.445 m, filters B-10,Al (permanent), Mn,Co,Pd,     21522  1   47 
             W,Ta (background)                                    21522  1   48 
DETECTOR   (SIBAR) 2 Si(Au)-surface barrier detectors, 20 cm*cm   21522  1   49 
            sensitive area (ORTEC). Both detectors at 90. degr    21522  1   50 
            with respect to the neutron beam.                     21522  1   51 
MONITOR    (92-U-235(N,F),,SIG) 2200 m/sec cross section value.   21522  1   52 
            All the fission integrals used correspond to a 2200   21522  1   53 
            m/sec value of 587.6+-2.6 barn.                       21522  1   54 
            Below 30 eV normalization is done with respect to the 21522  1   55 
            fission integral between 0.0206 and 0.06239 eV, with  21522  1   56 
            a value of 19.26 +- 0.08 B*eV.                        21522  1   57 
            Above 30 eV normalization is done with respect to the 21522  1   58 
            fission integral between 100. and 200. eV, with a     21522  1   59 
            value of 2144. +- 30. b*eV.                           21522  1   60 
MONIT-REF  (20143002,A.J.Deruytter+,J,JNE,27,(9),645,197309)      21522  1   61 
COMMENT     Assumption of 1/V shape of Li-6 and B-10 cross        21522  1   62 
            sections can easily be corrected for.                 21522  1   63 
            Errors due to fission fragment backscattering         21522  1   64 
            and anisotropy effects in the (n,alpha) reactions are 21522  1   65 
            zero.                                                 21522  1   66 
            Error above 30 eV is greater because of a 2 steps     21522  1   67 
            normalization procedure.                              21522  1   68 
            Data compared with results of other authors in        21522  1   69 
            Tables 2-6 of Knoxville article.                      21522  1   70 
            This comparison is qualitatively still valid since    21522  1   71 
            the fission integrals are not very much affected      21522  1   72 
            by the error found in the computer code ANGELA.       21522  1   73 
STATUS     (TABLE) Data taken from 79KNOX,,961,1979 and prev.comm.21522  1   74 
CORRECTION  Background (fits of black resonance data).            21522  1   75 
            background amounts to less than 0.5% in the           21522  1   76 
            thermal energy region and increases to 1-2%           21522  1   77 
            in the eV-region.                                     21522  1   78 
ERR-ANALYS (DATA-ERR) Overall total error of 1.5% below 30. eV    21522  1   79 
            3.0% above 30. eV. The uncertainty includes           21522  1   80 
            statistical uncertainties (also from background       21522  1   81 
            spectra), the error of the normalization(S), the      21522  1   82 
            systematic error of the background fits, the error    21522  1   83 
            on the energy interval bounds (for the fission        21522  1   84 
            integrals).                                           21522  1   85
